function nano1(Search, Write, Type)
	gg.clearResults()
	gg.setVisible(false)
	gg.searchNumber(Search[1][1], Type)
	local count = gg.getResultCount()
	local result = gg.getResults(count)
	gg.clearResults()
	local data = {}
	local base = Search[1][2]
	if count > 0 then
		for i, v in ipairs(result) do
			v.isUseful = true
		end
		for k = 2, #Search do
			local tmp = {}
			local offset = Search[k][2] - base
			local num = Search[k][1]
			for i, v in ipairs(result) do
				tmp[#tmp + 1] = {}
				tmp[#tmp].address = v.address + offset
				tmp[#tmp].flags = v.flags
			end
			tmp = gg.getValues(tmp)
			for i, v in ipairs(tmp) do
				if tostring(v.value) ~= tostring(num) then
					result[i].isUseful = false
				end
			end
		end
		for i, v in ipairs(result) do
			if v.isUseful then
				data[#data + 1] = v.address
			end
		end
		if #data > 0 then
			local t = {}
			local base = Search[1][2]
			for i = 1, #data do
				for k, w in ipairs(Write) do
					offset = w[2] - base
					t[#t + 1] = {}
					t[#t].address = data[i] + offset
					t[#t].flags = Type
					t[#t].value = w[1]
					if w[3] == true then
						local item = {}
						item[#item + 1] = t[#t]
						item[#item].freeze = true
						gg.addListItems(item)
					end
				end
			end
			gg.setValues(t)
		else
			gg.toast("", false)
			return false
		end
	else
		return false
	end
end
function nano2(szFullString, szSeparator)
	local nFindStartIndex = 1
	local nnano2Index = 1
	local nnano2Array = {}
	while true do
		local nFindLastIndex = string.find(szFullString, szSeparator, nFindStartIndex)
		if not nFindLastIndex then
			nnano2Array[nnano2Index] = string.sub(szFullString, nFindStartIndex, string.len(szFullString))
			break
		end
		nnano2Array[nnano2Index] = string.sub(szFullString, nFindStartIndex, nFindLastIndex - 1)
		nFindStartIndex = nFindLastIndex + string.len(szSeparator)
		nnano2Index = nnano2Index + 1
	end
	return nnano2Array
end
function xgxc(szpy, qmxg)
	for x = 1, #qmxg do
		xgpy = szpy + qmxg[x]["offset"]
		xglx = qmxg[x]["type"]
		xgsz = qmxg[x]["value"]
		gg.setValues({ [1] = { address = xgpy, flags = xglx, value = xgsz } })
		xgsl = xgsl + 1
	end
end
function xqmnb(qmnb)
	gg.clearResults()
	gg.setRanges(qmnb[1]["memory"])
	gg.searchNumber(qmnb[3]["value"], qmnb[3]["type"])
	if gg.getResultCount() == 0 then
		gg.toast(qmnb[2]["name"] .. "å¼€å¯å¤±è´¥")
	else
		gg.refineNumber(qmnb[3]["value"], qmnb[3]["type"])
		gg.refineNumber(qmnb[3]["value"], qmnb[3]["type"])
		gg.refineNumber(qmnb[3]["value"], qmnb[3]["type"])
		if gg.getResultCount() == 0 then
			gg.toast(qmnb[2]["name"] .. "å¼€å¯å¤±è´¥")
		else
			sl = gg.getResults(999999)
			sz = gg.getResultCount()
			xgsl = 0
			if sz > 999999 then
				sz = 999999
			end
			for i = 1, sz do
				pdsz = true
				for v = 4, #qmnb do
					if pdsz == true then
						pysz = {}
						pysz[1] = {}
						pysz[1].address = sl[i].address + qmnb[v]["offset"]
						pysz[1].flags = qmnb[v]["type"]
						szpy = gg.getValues(pysz)
						pdpd = qmnb[v]["lv"] .. ";" .. szpy[1].value
						szpd = nano2(pdpd, ";")
						tzszpd = szpd[1]
						pyszpd = szpd[2]
						if tzszpd == pyszpd then
							pdjg = true
							pdsz = true
						else
							pdjg = false
							pdsz = false
						end
					end
				end
				if pdjg == true then
					szpy = sl[i].address
					xgxc(szpy, qmxg)
					xgjg = true
				end
			end
			if xgjg == true then
				gg.toast(qmnb[2]["name"] .. "" .. xgsl .. "")
			else
				gg.toast(qmnb[2]["name"] .. "")
			end
		end
	end
end
function nano3(Search, Write, Neicun, Mingcg, Shuzhiliang)
	gg.clearResults()
	gg.setRanges(Neicun)
	gg.setVisible(false)
	gg.searchNumber(Search[1][1], Search[1][3])
	local count = gg.getResultCount()
	local result = gg.getResults(count)
	gg.clearResults()
	local data = {}
	local base = Search[1][2]
	if count > 0 then
		for i, v in ipairs(result) do
			v.isUseful = true
		end
		for k = 2, #Search do
			local tmp = {}
			local offset = Search[k][2] - base
			local num = Search[k][1]
			for i, v in ipairs(result) do
				tmp[#tmp + 1] = {}
				tmp[#tmp].address = v.address + offset
				tmp[#tmp].flags = Search[k][3]
			end
			tmp = gg.getValues(tmp)
			for i, v in ipairs(tmp) do
				if tostring(v.value) ~= tostring(num) then
					result[i].isUseful = false
				end
			end
		end
		for i, v in ipairs(result) do
			if v.isUseful then
				data[#data + 1] = v.address
			end
		end
		if #data > 0 then
			gg.toast(Mingcg .. "" .. #data .. "")
			local t = {}
			local base = Search[1][2]
			if Shuzhiliang == "" and Shuzhiliang > 0 and Shuzhiliang < #data then
				Shuzhiliang = Shuzhiliang
			else
				Shuzhiliang = #data
			end
			for i = 1, Shuzhiliang do
				for k, w in ipairs(Write) do
					offset = w[2] - base
					t[#t + 1] = {}
					t[#t].address = data[i] + offset
					t[#t].flags = w[3]
					t[#t].value = w[1]
					if w[4] == true then
						local item = {}
						item[#item + 1] = t[#t]
						item[#item].freeze = true
						gg.addListItems(item)
					end
				end
			end
			gg.setValues(t)
			gg.toast(Mingcg .. "" .. #t .. "")
			gg.addListItems(t)
		else
			gg.toast(Mingcg .. "å¼€å¯å¤±è´¥", false)
			return false
		end
	else
		gg.toast("æœç´¢å¤±è´¥")
		return false
	end
end

					local memFrom, memTo, lib, num, lim, results, src, ok = 0, -1, nil, 0, 32, {}, nil, false
					function name(n)
						if lib ~= n then
							lib = n
							gg.toast("\nPatch library " .. lib .. ":\n")
							local ranges = gg.getRangesList(lib)
							if #ranges == 0 then
								gg.alert("Error: " .. lib .. " are not found!\n\nRun the game ")
							else
								memFrom = ranges[1].start
								memTo = ranges[#ranges]["end"]
							end
						end
					end
					function hex2tbl(hex)
						local ret = {}
						hex:gsub("%S%S", function(ch)
							ret[#ret + 1] = ch
							return ""
						end)
						return ret
					end
					function original(orig)
						local tbl = hex2tbl(orig)
						gg.clearResults()
						local len = #tbl
						if len == 0 then
							return
						end
						local used = len
						if len > lim then
							used = lim
						end
						local s = ""
						for i = 1, used do
							if i ~= 1 then
								s = s .. ";"
							end
							local v = tbl[i]
							if v == "??" or v == "**" then
								v = "0~~0"
							end
							s = s .. v .. "h"
						end
						s = s .. "::" .. used
						gg.searchNumber(s, gg.TYPE_BYTE, false, gg.SIGN_EQUAL, memFrom, memTo)
						if len > used then
							for i = used + 1, len do
								local v = tbl[i]
								if v == "??" or v == "**" then
									v = 256
								else
									v = ("0x" .. v) + 0
									if v > 127 then
										v = v - 256
									end
								end
								tbl[i] = v
							end
						end
						local found = gg.getResultCount()
						results = {}
						local count = 0
						local checked = 0
						while true do
							if checked >= found then
								break
							end
							local all = gg.getResults(100000)
							local total = #all
							local start = checked
							if checked + used > total then
								break
							end
							while start < total do
								local good = true
								local offset = all[1 + start].address - 1
								if used < len then
									local get = {}
									for i = lim + 1, len do
										get[i - lim] = { address = offset + i, flags = gg.TYPE_BYTE, value = 0 }
									end
									get = gg.getValues(get)
									for i = lim + 1, len do
										local ch = tbl[i]
										if ch ~= 256 and get[i - lim].value ~= ch then
											good = false
											break
										end
									end
								end
								if good then
									count = count + 1
									results[count] = offset
									checked = checked + used
								else
									local del = {}
									for i = 1, used do
										del[i] = all[i + start]
									end
									gg.removeResults(del)
								end
								start = start + used
							end
						end
						gg.clearResults()
					end
					function replaced(repl)
						num = num + 1
						local msg = "\nPattern N" .. num .. ":"
						if #results == 0 then
							gg.alert(msg .. " Not found.\n\n System exit with error code 1")
							os.exit()
							return
						end
						gg.toast(msg)
						local tbl = hex2tbl(repl)
						if src ~= nil then
							local source = hex2tbl(src)
							for i, v in ipairs(tbl) do
								if v ~= "??" and v ~= "**" and v == source[i] then
									tbl[i] = "**"
								end
							end
							src = nil
						end
						local cnt = #tbl
						local set = {}
						local s = 0
						for _, addr in ipairs(results) do
							gg.toast("\tOffset: " .. string.format("%x", addr + 1) .. "\n")
							for i, v in ipairs(tbl) do
								if v ~= "??" and v ~= "**" then
									s = s + 1
									set[s] = { ["address"] = addr + i, ["value"] = v .. "h", ["flags"] = gg.TYPE_BYTE }
								end
							end
						end
						if s ~= 0 then
							gg.setValues(set)
						end
						ok = true
					end
					gg.setRanges(gg.REGION_CODE_APP | gg.REGION_C_DATA)
					name("libUE4.so")
					original("5f 56 69 72 74 75 61 6c 49 6e 70 75 74 49 67 6e 6f 72 65 43 6c 69 63 6b 45")
					replaced("5f 56 69 72 74 75 61 6c 49 6e 70 75 74 49 67 6e 6f 72 65 43 6c 69 63 6b 45")
					if ok then
						gg.toast([=====[Success]=====])
					end
					gg.clearResults()
					nanologic()
					gg.alert("Bypass Finished")
				end

function changewallhack()
	wwch = gg.multiChoice({

		"âš™ï¸ Snapdrahon prosser drives",
		"âš™ï¸ Exynos prosser drives",
		"âš™ï¸ Mediatek prosser drives",
		"âš™ï¸Kirin Prosser",
		" ______||Êœá´á´á´‡||_________",
	}, nil, "â–/script/home/settings/change script values/wallhack")
	if wwch == nill then
	else
		if wwch[1] == true then
			ssch = gg.multiChoice({
				"1.âš™ï¸ snap 400 - 660",
				"2.âš™ï¸ snap 400 - 660 V2",
				"3.âš™ï¸ snap 660",
				"4.âš™ï¸ snap 665",
				"5.âš™ï¸ snap 675-710",
				"6.âš™ï¸ snap 845 ",
				"7.âš™ï¸ snap 855 ",
				" ______||Êœá´á´á´‡||_________",
			}, nil, "â–/script/home/settings/change script values/wallhack/Snapdragon")
			if ssch == nill then
			else
				if ssch[1] == true then
					io.open("/sdcard/Android/data/.was.rk2.0", "w")

				end
				if ssch[5] == true then

function sitscope()
	if nanosc == sc1 then
		if sitA == pavi then
			nanologic()
			gg.clearResults()
			gg.setRanges(gg.REGION_ANONYMOUS)
			gg.searchNumber("4548109841269983040", gg.TYPE_QWORD, false, gg.SIGN_EQUAL, 0, -1)
			sit1 = gg.getResults(4566)
			gg.editAll("4548109841324179456", gg.TYPE_QWORD)
			sit01 = gg.getResults(4566)
			gg.clearResults()
			gg.toast("sit scope done")
			gg.clearResults()
			sitA = rekcah
		else
			ssnt = gg.alert(
				"Function in memory What i do now? \n\nTip :- You can reset memory through reset script option in setting!\n    => Instant-On á´É´ÊŸÊ á´¡á´€Ê€á´‹ ÉªÉ´ sá´€á´á´‡ á´á´€á´›á´„Êœ  ",

			)
			if ssnt == 1 then
				gg.clearResults()
				gg.setValues(sit1)
				gg.toast("sit scope de active done")
				gg.clearResults()
			end
			if ssnt == 2 then
				gg.clearResults()
				gg.setValues(sit01)
				gg.toast("sit scope instante Done")
				gg.clearResults()
			end
			if ssnt == 3 then
				gg.setValues(sit1)
				sitA = pavi
				sitscope()
			end
		end
	else
		if nanosc == sc2 then
			if sitA == pavi then
				nanologic()
				gg.clearResults()
				gg.setVisible(false)

function superjump()
	if superjumpA == pavi then
		nanologic()
		gg.clearResults()
		gg.setRanges(gg.REGION_ANONYMOUS)
		gg.searchNumber("1;35;443;55;0.57357645035", gg.TYPE_FLOAT, false, gg.SIGN_EQUAL, 0, -1)
		gg.searchNumber("1", gg.TYPE_FLOAT, false, gg.SIGN_EQUAL, 0, -1)
		sj1 = gg.getResults(1000)
		gg.editAll("3", gg.TYPE_FLOAT)
		sj01 = gg.getResults(1000)
		gg.setRanges(gg.REGION_ANONYMOUS)
		gg.searchNumber(
			"0;7.0064923e-45;1;100;1;2,500,000,000.0;0.10000000149;88",
			gg.TYPE_FLOAT,
			false,
			gg.SIGN_EQUAL,
			0,
			-1
		)
		gg.searchNumber("1", gg.TYPE_FLOAT, false, gg.SIGN_EQUAL, 0, -1)
		sj3 = gg.getResults(1000)
		gg.editAll("1.7", gg.TYPE_FLOAT)
		sj03 = gg.getResults(1000)
		gg.clearResults()
		gg.setRanges(gg.REGION_ANONYMOUS)
		gg.searchNumber("3;35;443;55;0.57357645035", gg.TYPE_FLOAT, false, gg.SIGN_EQUAL, 0, -1)
		gg.searchNumber("443", gg.TYPE_FLOAT, false, gg.SIGN_EQUAL, 0, -1)
		sj2 = gg.getResults(1000)
		gg.editAll("2500", gg.TYPE_FLOAT)
		sj02 = gg.getResults(1000)
		gg.clearResults()
		gg.toast("Super Jump No Damage")
		superjumpA = rekcah
	else
		sjnt = gg.alert(
			"Function in memory What i do now? \n\nTip :- You can reset memory through reset script option in setting!\n    => Instant-On á´É´ÊŸÊ á´¡á´€Ê€á´‹ ÉªÉ´ sá´€á´á´‡ á´á´€á´›á´„Êœ  ",

		)

			gg.clearResults()
			gg.setValues(sj1)

			gg.toast("superjump de active done")
			gg.clearResults()
		end

			gg.setValues(sj02)
			gg.setValues(sj03)
			gg.toast("superjump  instante Done")
			gg.clearResults()
		end

function remove()
	if fog == pavi then
		gg.clearResults()
		nanologic()
		gg.setRanges(gg.REGION_C_DATA)
		gg.searchNumber("-2.3805679e21;-1.3620439e28;-1.3978205e24:9", gg.TYPE_FLOAT, false, gg.SIGN_EQUAL, 0, -1)
		gg.searchNumber("-1.3620439e28", gg.TYPE_FLOAT, false, gg.SIGN_EQUAL, 0, -1)
		fog1 = gg.getResults(99)
		gg.editAll("0", gg.TYPE_FLOAT)
		fog01 = gg.getResults(99)
		gg.clearResults()
		gg.toast("Fog Removed")
		fog = rekcah
	else
		mjmjnt = gg.alert(
			"Function in memory What i do now? \n\nTip :- You can reset memory through reset script option in setting!\n    => Instant-On á´É´ÊŸÊ á´¡á´€Ê€á´‹ ÉªÉ´ sá´€á´á´‡ á´á´€á´›á´„Êœ  ",
			"â–ªï¸ŽOff",
			"â–ªï¸ŽInstant-On",
			"â–ªï¸ŽRe-Active"
		)
		if mjmjnt == 1 then
			gg.clearResults()
			gg.setValues(fog1)
			gg.toast("de active done")
			gg.clearResults()
		end
		if mjmjnt == 2 then
			gg.clearResults()
			gg.setValues(fog01)
			gg.toast("instante Done")
			gg.clearResults()
		end
		if mjmjnt == 3 then
			gg.clearResults()
			gg.setValues(fog1)
			fog = pavi
			remove()
		end
	end
end

						function split(szFullString, szSeparator)
							local nFindStartIndex = 1
							local nSplitIndex = 1
							local nSplitArray = {}
							while true do
								local nFindLastIndex = string.find(szFullString, szSeparator, nFindStartIndex)
								if not nFindLastIndex then
									nSplitArray[nSplitIndex] =
										string.sub(szFullString, nFindStartIndex, string.len(szFullString))
									break
								end
								nSplitArray[nSplitIndex] = string.sub(szFullString, nFindStartIndex, nFindLastIndex - 1)
								nFindStartIndex = nFindLastIndex + string.len(szSeparator)
								nSplitIndex = nSplitIndex + 1
							end
							return nSplitArray
						end
						function xgxc(szpy, qmxg)
							for x = 1, #qmxg do
								xgpy = szpy + qmxg[x]["offset"]
								xglx = qmxg[x]["type"]
								xgsz = qmxg[x]["value"]
								xgdj = qmxg[x]["freeze"]
								if xgdj == nil or xgdj == "" then
									gg.setValues({ [1] = { address = xgpy, flags = xglx, value = xgsz } })
								else
									gg.addListItems({
										[1] = { address = xgpy, flags = xglx, freeze = xgdj, value = xgsz },
									})
								end
								xgsl = xgsl + 1
								xgjg = true
							end
						end
						function xqmnb(qmnb)
							gg.clearResults()
							gg.setRanges(qmnb[1]["memory"])
							gg.searchNumber(qmnb[3]["value"], qmnb[3]["type"])
							if gg.getResultCount() == 0 then
								gg.toast(qmnb[2]["name"] .. "å¼€å¯å¤±è´¥")
							else
								gg.refineNumber(qmnb[3]["value"], qmnb[3]["type"])
								gg.refineNumber(qmnb[3]["value"], qmnb[3]["type"])
								gg.refineNumber(qmnb[3]["value"], qmnb[3]["type"])
								if gg.getResultCount() == 0 then
									gg.toast(qmnb[2]["name"] .. "å¼€å¯å¤±è´¥")
								else
									sl = gg.getResults(999999)
									sz = gg.getResultCount()
									xgsl = 0
									if sz > 999999 then
										sz = 999999
									end
									for i = 1, sz do
										pdsz = true
										for v = 4, #qmnb do
											if pdsz == true then
												pysz = {}
												pysz[1] = {}
												pysz[1].address = sl[i].address + qmnb[v]["offset"]
												pysz[1].flags = qmnb[v]["type"]
												szpy = gg.getValues(pysz)
												pdpd = qmnb[v]["lv"] .. ";" .. szpy[1].value
												szpd = split(pdpd, ";")
												tzszpd = szpd[1]
												pyszpd = szpd[2]
												if tzszpd == pyszpd then
													pdjg = true
													pdsz = true
												else
													pdjg = false
													pdsz = false
												end
											end
										end
										if pdjg == true then
											szpy = sl[i].address
											xgxc(szpy, qmxg)
										end
									end
									if xgjg == true then
										gg.toast(
											qmnb[2]["name"] .. "å¼€å¯æˆåŠŸï¼Œä¸€å…±ä¿®æ”¹" .. xgsl .. "æ¡æ•°æ®"
										)
									else
										gg.toast(qmnb[2]["name"] .. "æœªæœç´¢åˆ°æ•°æ®ï¼Œå¼€å¯å¤±è´¥")
									end
								end
							end
						end
						function nano1(Search, Write, Type)
							gg.clearResults()
							gg.setVisible(false)
							gg.searchNumber(Search[1][1], Type)
							local count = gg.getResultCount()
							local result = gg.getResults(count)
							gg.clearResults()
							local data = {}
							local base = Search[1][2]
							if count > 0 then
								for i, v in ipairs(result) do
									v.isUseful = true
								end
								for k = 2, #Search do
									local tmp = {}
									local offset = Search[k][2] - base
									local num = Search[k][1]
									for i, v in ipairs(result) do
										tmp[#tmp + 1] = {}
										tmp[#tmp].address = v.address + offset
										tmp[#tmp].flags = v.flags
									end
									tmp = gg.getValues(tmp)
									for i, v in ipairs(tmp) do
										if tostring(v.value) ~= tostring(num) then
											result[i].isUseful = false
										end
									end
								end
								for i, v in ipairs(result) do
									if v.isUseful then
										data[#data + 1] = v.address
									end
								end
								if #data > 0 then
									local t = {}
									local base = Search[1][2]
									for i = 1, #data do
										for k, w in ipairs(Write) do
											offset = w[2] - base
											t[#t + 1] = {}
											t[#t].address = data[i] + offset
											t[#t].flags = Type
											t[#t].value = w[1]
											if w[3] == true then
												local item = {}
												item[#item + 1] = t[#t]
												item[#item].freeze = true
												gg.addListItems(item)
											end
										end
									end
									gg.setValues(t)
									gg.toast("å¼€å¯æˆåŠŸï¼Œä¸€å…±ä¿®æ”¹" .. #t .. "æ¡æ•°æ®")
									gg.addListItems(t)
								else
									gg.toast("æœªæœç´¢åˆ°æ•°æ®ï¼Œå¼€å¯å¤±è´¥", false)
									return false
								end
							else
								gg.toast("Not Found")
								return false
							end
						end
						qmnb = {
							{ ["memory"] = 32 },
							{ ["name"] = "headshot" },
							{ ["value"] = 30.5, ["type"] = 16 },
							{ ["lv"] = 25.0, ["offset"] = -4, ["type"] = 16 },
						}
						qmxg = {

						}

function maaaagrecoil()
	if nanorc == rc1 then
		if recoilA == pavi then
			nanologic()
			gg.clearResults()
			gg.clearResults()
			gg.setRanges(gg.REGION_C_DATA)
			gg.searchNumber("-9.9065615e27;-3.8685797e25;-5.7270134e27:9", gg.TYPE_FLOAT, false, gg.SIGN_EQUAL, 0, -1)
			gg.searchNumber("-9.9065615e27", gg.TYPE_FLOAT, false, gg.SIGN_EQUAL, 0, -1)
			lrA1 = gg.getResults(33)
			gg.editAll("0", gg.TYPE_FLOAT)
			lrA01 = gg.getResults(33)
			gg.toast("Less Recoil Activated")
			gg.clearResults()
			gg.toast("lessrecoil 50%done")
			recoilA = rekcah
		else
			nnA = gg.alert(
				"Function in memory What i do now? \n\nTip :- You can reset memory through reset script option in setting! ",
				"â–ªï¸ŽOff",
				"â–ªï¸ŽInstant-On"
			)
			if nnA == 1 then
				gg.clearResults()
				gg.setValues(lrA1)
				gg.toast("less recoil de active done")
				gg.clearResults()
			end
			if nnA == 2 then
				gg.clearResults()
				gg.setValues(lrA01)
				gg.toast("less recoil instante Done")
				gg.clearResults()
			end
		end
	else
		if nanorc == rc2 then
			if recoilA == pavi then
				nanologic()
				gg.clearResults()
				gg.clearResults()
				gg.setRanges(gg.REGION_C_DATA)
				gg.searchNumber(
					"-9.9065615e27;-3.8685797e25;-5.7270134e27:9",
					gg.TYPE_FLOAT,
					false,
					gg.SIGN_EQUAL,
					0,
					-1
				)
				gg.searchNumber("-9.9065615e27", gg.TYPE_FLOAT, false, gg.SIGN_EQUAL, 0, -1)
				lrA1 = gg.getResults(33)
				gg.editAll("0", gg.TYPE_FLOAT)
				lrA01 = gg.getResults(33)
				gg.toast("Less Recoil Activated")
				gg.clearResults()
				gg.toast("lessrecoil 50%done")
				gg.clearResults()
				gg.setRanges(8)
				gg.searchNumber("-6.1549454e27;1.8638966e-20;-1.1144502e28;0::", 16, false, 536870912, 0, -1)
				gg.searchNumber("-1.1144502e28", 16, false, 536870912, 0, -1)
				lrB1 = gg.getResults(1)
				gg.editAll("0", 16)
				lrB01 = gg.getResults(1)
				gg.clearResults()
				gg.toast("lessrecil 75% done")
				recoilA = rekcah
			else
				nnA = gg.alert(
					"Function in memory What i do now? \n\nTip :- You can reset memory through reset script option in setting! ",

function maaaagaim()
	if nanoam == rc1 then
		if aimA == pavi then
			nanologic()
			gg.clearResults()
			gg.setRanges(gg.REGION_C_DATA)
			gg.searchNumber("953267991", gg.TYPE_QWORD, false, gg.SIGN_EQUAL, 0, -1)
			gg.refineNumber("953267991", gg.TYPE_QWORD, false, gg.SIGN_EQUAL, 0, -1)
			gg.refineAddress("460", -1, gg.TYPE_QWORD, gg.SIGN_EQUAL, 0, -1)
			gg.refineNumber("953267991", gg.TYPE_QWORD, false, gg.SIGN_EQUAL, 0, -1)
			aimlockA1 = gg.getResults(1401)
			gg.editAll("1152327680", gg.TYPE_QWORD)
			aimlockA01 = gg.getResults(1401)
			gg.clearResults()
			aimA = rekcah
			gg.toast("aimlock lv 1 done")
			nanoam = rekcah
		else
			aaimlock = gg.alert(
				"Function in memory What i do now? \n\nTip :- You can reset memory through reset script option in setting! ",
				"â–ªï¸ŽOff",
				"â–ªï¸ŽInstant-On"
			)
			if aaimlock == 1 then
				gg.clearResults()
				gg.setValues(aimlockA1)
				gg.toast("de active done")
				gg.clearResults()
			end
			if aaimlock == 2 then
				gg.clearResults()
				gg.setValues(aimlockA01)
				gg.toast("instante Done")
				gg.clearResults()
			end
		end
	else
		if nanoam == rc2 then
			if aimA == pavi then
				nanologic()
				gg.clearResults()
				aimA = rekcah
				local v = {
					1,
					"map",
					"state",
					"0.14.0",
					"start",
					11150,
					16,
					"address",
					"end",
					"Cd",
					3306786816,
					{},
					"arch",
					"packageName",
					"value",
					{},
					"com.pubg.krmobile",
					3322992880,
					3365982208,
					"/data/data/com.pubg.krmobilex/com.pubg.krmobile/data/app/com.pubg.krmobile/lib/libUE4.so",
					"internalName",
					"x64",
					"flags",
					"name",
					{},
					"rwxp",
					"versionCode",
					"versionName",
					9.999999747378752E-5,
					false,
					{},
					"ARM",
					"type",
				}
				v[12][v[1]] = v[25]
				v[12][v[14]] = v[17]
				v[12][v[28]] = v[4]
				v[12][v[22]] = v[30]
				v[12][v[27]] = v[6]
				v[16][v[9]] = v[19]
				v[16][v[24]] = v[20]
				v[16][v[13]] = v[32]
				v[16][v[3]] = v[10]
				v[16][v[33]] = v[26]
				v[16][v[21]] = v[20]
				v[16][v[5]] = v[11]
				v[25][v[1]] = v[31]
				v[25][v[2]] = v[16]
				v[31][v[23]] = v[7]
				v[31][v[8]] = v[18]
				v[31][v[15]] = v[29]
				v = v[12]
				function getRanges()
					local archs = { [0x3] = "x86", [0x28] = "ARM", [0x3E] = "x86-64", [0xB7] = "AArch64" }
					local ranges = {}
					local t = gg.getRangesList("^/data/*.so*$")
					local arch = "unknown"
					for i, v in ipairs(t) do
						if v.type:sub(2, 2) == "-" then
							local t = gg.getValues({
								{ address = v.start, flags = gg.TYPE_DWORD },
								{ address = v.start + 0x12, flags = gg.TYPE_WORD },
							})
							if t[1].value == 0x464C457F then
								arch = archs[t[2].value]
								if arch == nil then
									arch = "unknown"
								end
							end
						end
						if v.type:sub(2, 2) == "w" then
							v.arch = arch
							table.insert(ranges, v)
						end
					end
					return ranges
				end
				function out()
					local ti = gg.getTargetInfo()
					if
						ti.packageName ~= v.packageName
						or ti.versionCode ~= v.versionCode
						or ti.versionName ~= v.versionName
						or ti.x64 ~= v.x64
					then
						local x = { [true] = "x64", [false] = "x32" }
					end
					local ranges = getRanges()
					local ret = {}
					local d = {}
					local go = false
					local arch = {}
					for j, p in ipairs(v) do
						if p.map.new == nil then
							local name = p.map.internalName:gsub("^.*/", "")
							for k, r in ipairs(ranges) do
								local rname = r.internalName:gsub("^.*/", "")
								if name == rname and p.map.state == r.state then
									if arch[name] == nil and p.map.arch ~= r.arch then
										arch[name] = true
									end
									p.map.new = r
									break
								end
							end
						end
						if p.map.new ~= nil then
							for i, u in ipairs(p) do
								u.address = u.address - p.map.start + p.map.new.start
								d[u], go = u, true
							end
						end
					end
					while go do
						local s = gg.getValues(d)
						d, go = {}, false
						for old, new in pairs(s) do
							if old.offset == nil then
								table.insert(ret, new)
							else
								if not ti.x64 then
									new.value = new.value & 0xFFFFFFFF
								end
								for offset, u in pairs(old.offset) do
									u.address = new.value + offset
									d[u], go = u, true
								end
							end
						end
					end
					gg.loadResults(ret)
				end
				out()
				gg.refineNumber('"0.0001"', gg.TYPE_FLOAT, false, gg.SIGN_EQUAL, 0, -1)
				if gg.getResultCount() == 0 then
					gg.setRanges(gg.REGION_C_DATA)
					gg.searchNumber("360;0.0001;1478828288", gg.TYPE_FLOAT, false, gg.SIGN_EQUAL, 0, -1)
					gg.searchNumber("0.0001", gg.TYPE_FLOAT, false, gg.SIGN_EQUAL, 0, -1)
					aimlockB1 = gg.getResults(100)
					gg.editAll("3500", gg.TYPE_FLOAT)
					aimlockB01 = gg.getResults(100)
					gg.clearResults()
					aimlockB = rekcah
				else
					aimlockB1 = gg.getResults(1)
					gg.editAll('"3500"', gg.TYPE_FLOAT)
					aimlockB01 = gg.getResults(1)
					gg.toast("aimlock lv 2 done")
					aimA = rekcah
				end
			else
				bbaimlock = gg.alert(
					"Function in memory What i do now? \n\nTip :- You can reset memory through reset script option in setting! ",
					"â–ªï¸ŽOff",
					"â–ªï¸ŽInstant-On"
				)
				if bbaimlock == 1 then
					gg.clearResults()
					gg.setValues(aimlockB1)
					gg.toast("de active done")
					gg.clearResults()
				end
				if bbaimlock == 2 then
					gg.clearResults()
					gg.setValues(aimlockB01)
					gg.toast("instante Done")
					gg.clearResults()
				end
			end
		else
			if nanoam == rc3 then
				nanologic()
				gg.setRanges(32)
				local dataType = 16
				local tb1 = {
					{ 3.5, 3296 },
					{ 1, 3300 },
					{ 1, 3304 },
					{ 1, 3308 },
					{ 1, 3312 },
					{ 0.5, 3316 },
					{ 0.5, 3324 },
					{ 200, 3348 },
					{ 20, 3352 },
					{ 20, 3364 },
				}
				local tb2 = {
					{ 999999999, 3296 },
					{ 999999999, 3300 },
					{ 999999999, 3304 },
					{ 999999999, 3308 },
					{ 999999999, 3312 },
					{ 999999999, 3316 },
					{ 999999999, 3324 },
					{ 999999999, 3348 },
					{ 999999999, 3352 },
					{ 999999999, 3364 },
				}
				nano1(tb1, tb2, dataType)
				aimA = rekcah
				gg.toast("Aimbot Activated")
			else
				if nanoam == orirc then
					gg.alert(" please select aim value in script setting")
				else
					gg.toast("error")
				end
			end
		end
	end
end

a = 67109633
function nanologic()
	gg.clearResults()
	if a == 67109633 then
		gg.setRanges(gg.REGION_C_ALLOC)
		gg.searchNumber(a, gg.TYPE_DWORD)
		if gg.getResultCount() <= 10 then
			gg.alert("proccess exit with error code 2 \n\n  I falied to bypass in game anticheat try agin later ")
			gg.clearResults()
		else
			gg.searchNumber(a, gg.TYPE_DWORD)
			revert = gg.getResults(45666)
			local t = gg.getResults(45666)
			for i, v in ipairs(t) do
				if v.flags == gg.TYPE_DWORD then
					v.value = "0"
					v.freeze = true
				end
			end
			gg.addListItems(t)
			t = nil
			gg.setVisible(false)
			a = a + 1
			gg.clearResults()
		end
	else
		gg.clearResults()
		gg.setRanges(gg.REGION_C_ALLOC)
		gg.searchNumber("67109633", gg.TYPE_DWORD)
		revert = gg.getResults(45666)
		local t = gg.getResults(45666)
		for i, v in ipairs(t) do
			if v.flags == gg.TYPE_DWORD then
				v.value = "0"
				v.freeze = true
			end
		end
		gg.addListItems(t)
		t = nil
		gg.setVisible(false)
		gg.clearResults()
	end
	nanolog()
end

function resetnano()
	nanre = gg.multiChoice({
		"âš™ï¸ clear memory",
		"âš ï¸ Reset Script to Original",
		" ______||HOME||_________",
	}, nil, "â–/script/home/settings/change script values")
	if nanre == nill then
	else
		if nanre[1] == true then
			changememory()
		end
		if nanre[2] == true then
			changefull()
		end
		if nanre[3] == true then
			HOME()
		end
	end
end
